= 190;\nconst MR = 80;\nconst MB = 110;\nconst ML = 110;\nconst CW = W - ML - MR;\nconst CH = H - MT - MB;\nconst BAR_GAP = 0.38;\nconst BAR_W = (CW / populationData.length) * (1 - BAR_GAP);\nconst Y_MIN = 1_300_000_000;\nconst Y_MAX = 1_430_000_000;\nconst Y_RNG = Y_MAX - Y_MIN;\n\nconst getY = (val: number) => MT + CH - ((val - Y_MIN) / Y_RNG) * CH;\n\nconst fmt = (n: number) => (n / 100_000_000).toFixed(2) + \"亿\";\n\nexport const ChinaPopulation: React.FC = () => {\n  const frame = useCurrentFrame();\n\n  const titleIn = interpolate(frame, [0, 30], [0, 1], { extrapolateLeft: \"clamp\", extrapolateRight: \"clamp\" });\n  const titleY = interpolate(frame, [0, 30], [-25, 0], { extrapolateRight: \"clamp\" });\n\n  return (\n    <AbsoluteFill\n      style={{\n        background: \"linear-gradient(145deg, #070712 0%, #111128 40%, #0a0a1a 100%)\",\n        fontFamily: \"'Noto Sans SC','Microsoft YaHei','PingFang SC',sans-serif\",\n        color: \"#fff\",\n      }}\n    >\n      <div\n        style={{\n          position: \"absolute\",\n          top: 45,\n          width: \"100%\",\n          textAlign: \"center\",\n          opacity: titleIn,\n 中国人口变化趋势\n        </h1>\n        <p style={{ fontSize: 18, color: \"#475569\", margin: \"10px 0 0\", letterSpacing: 2 }}>\n          China Population (2014-2025) · World Bank\n        </p>\n      </div>\n\n      <svg width={W} height={H} style={{ position: \"absolute\", top: 0, left: 0 }}>\n        <defs>\n          <linearGradient id=\"gRise\" x1=\"0\" y1=\"0\" x2=\"0\" y2=\"1\">\n </defs>\n\n        {[1.3, 1.35, 1.4, 1.45].map((v) => {\n          const y = getY(v * 1_000_000_000);\n          const op = interpolate(frame, [5, 25], [0, 1], { extrapolateLeft: \"clamp\",    {populationData.map((d, i) => {\n          const start = 25 + i * 9;\n          const delay = Math.max(0, frame - start);\n          const h = ((d.population - Y_MIN) / Y_RNG) * CH;\n          const y = getY(d.population);\n          const totalW = CW / populationData.length;\n          const x = ML + i * totalW + (totalW - BAR_W) / 2;\n\n          const grow = spring({ frame: delay, fps: textAnchor=\"middle\" fill=\"#e2e8f0\" fontSize={13} fontWeight={600}>\n                  {fmt(d.population)}\n                </text>\n              )}\n            </g>\n          );\n        })}\n\n        {populationData.map((d, i) => {\n          const start = 25 + i * 9;\n          const op = interpolate(frame, [start, start + 8], [0, 1], { extrapolateLeft: \"clamp\", extrapolateRight: false (default): looks like a native auto-playing animation\n   * - true: looks like a standard video player\n   */\n  controls?: boolean\n  /** Auto-play on mount (default true) */\n  autoPlay?: boolean\n  /** Loop playback (default true) */\n  loop?: boolean\n  /** Click to toggle play/pause when controls are hidden (default true) */\n  clickToPlay?: boolean\n  /** Show volume slider in control bar (only relevant when controls=true) */\n  showVolumeControls?: boolean\n}\n\nexport function RemotionPlayer({\n  component: componentName,\n  durationInFrames = 210,\n  fps = 30,\n  compositionWidth = 1920,\n  compositionHeight = 1080,\n  controls = true,\n  autoPlay = true,\n  loop = true,\n  clickToPlay = true,\n  showVolumeControls = false,\n}: Props) {\n  const mdxComponents = useMDXComponents()\n  const Comp = (mdxComponents[componentName] ??\n    (() => null)) as ComponentType\n\n  const [mounted, setMounted] = React.useState(false)\n\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    setMounted(true)\n  }, [])\n\n  // Show a placeholder during SSR to avoid hydration mismatch\n  if (!mounted) {\n    return (\n      <div\n        className=\"my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg\"\n        style={{ aspectRatio: `${compositionWidth}/${compositionHeight}` }}\n      >\n        <div className=\"flex h-full items-center justify-center bg-muted text-sm text-muted-foreground\">\n          Loading animation…\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    )\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg\">\n      <Player\n        component={Comp}\n        durationInFrames={durationInFrames}\n        fps={fps}\n        compositionWidth={compositionWidth}\n        compositionHeight={compositionHeight}\n        style={{ width: '100%', display: 'block' }}\n        controls={controls}\n        autoPlay={autoPlay}\n        loop={loop}\n        clickToPlay={controls ? false : clickToPlay}\n        showVolumeControls={showVolumeControls}\n      />\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n",

    ..._provideComponents(),
    ...props.components
  };
  return MDXLayout ? _jsx(MDXLayout, {

    })
  }) : _createMdxContent(props);
}

  default: MDXContent
